# Add Evaluation Metadata Field to Flipt (Proto + Go)

**Repository:** flipt-io/flipt
**Access Scope:** You may modify files in `rpc/flipt/evaluation/` (protobuf schema + generated code) and `internal/server/evaluation/` (Go server). You may read any other files to understand existing patterns.

## Context

Flipt is a feature flag platform built with Go and gRPC. Its API is defined in Protocol Buffer (`.proto`) files, with generated Go code alongside. The evaluation server constructs protobuf response objects returned to clients.

Operators have requested that evaluation responses include a `segment_match_type` field so clients can see whether the evaluation matched a segment using `ALL` (all constraints matched) or `ANY` (at least one constraint matched) logic. This information is already available in the evaluation flow but is not exposed in the response.

## Task

Add a `segment_match_type` string field to the evaluation responses. This requires changes to **both** the protobuf schema (`.proto` file) and the Go server code that constructs responses — a cross-language change.

**YOU MUST IMPLEMENT CODE CHANGES.**

### Requirements

1. **Protobuf schema change** — Add `string segment_match_type` to the `VariantEvaluationResponse` message in the evaluation proto file. Determine the next sequential tag by examining existing fields in the message. The value should be "ALL", "ANY", or "" (empty when no segment matched).

2. **Generated Go code change** — Add the corresponding `SegmentMatchType string` field and getter method to the Go generated code (`.pb.go` file). Match the exact patterns used by existing fields. Do NOT regenerate code with protoc — manually add the field.

3. **Server code change** — In the evaluation server, populate `SegmentMatchType` on the response after evaluation logic determines which rule matched. The evaluation must set this field for variant evaluations, and batch responses should include it too.

4. **Determine the source value** — The storage layer carries segment operator information on evaluation rules that indicates ALL vs ANY. Find this type and trace how the operator maps to the string values you need.

## Success Criteria

- Evaluation proto has `segment_match_type` field in `VariantEvaluationResponse`
- Generated Go code has matching `SegmentMatchType` field and getter
- Server code populates `SegmentMatchType` from the rule's segment operator
- Proto tag number is valid (no collision with existing fields)
- Changes span both proto and Go files (cross-language change)
- Go code compiles: `go build ./internal/server/evaluation/...`

    19→}

    27→}

message EvaluationResponse {
  string request_id = 1;
  string entity_id = 2;
  map<string, string> request_context = 3;
  bool match = 4;
  string flag_key = 5;
  string segment_key = 6 [deprecated = true];
  google.protobuf.Timestamp timestamp = 7;
  string value = 8;
  double request_duration_millis = 9;
  string attachment = 10;
  EvaluationReason reason = 11;
  string namespace_key = 12;
  repeated string segment_keys = 13;
}

enum EvaluationReason {
  UNKNOWN_EVALUATION_REASON = 0;
  FLAG_DISABLED_EVALUATION_REASON = 1;
  FLAG_NOT_FOUND_EVALUATION_REASON = 2;
  MATCH_EVALUATION_REASON = 3;

type Flag struct {
	state         protoimpl.MessageState
	sizeCache     protoimpl.SizeCache
	unknownFields protoimpl.UnknownFields

	Key          string                 `protobuf:"bytes,1,opt,name=key,proto3" json:"key,omitempty"`
	Name         string                 `protobuf:"bytes,2,opt,name=name,proto3" json:"name,omitempty"`
	Description  string                 `protobuf:"bytes,3,opt,name=description,proto3" json:"description,omitempty"`
	Enabled      bool                   `protobuf:"varint,4,opt,name=enabled,proto3" json:"enabled,omitempty"`
	CreatedAt    *timestamppb.Timestamp `protobuf:"bytes,5,opt,name=created_at,json=createdAt,proto3" json:"created_at,omitempty"`
	UpdatedAt    *timestamppb.Timestamp `protobuf:"bytes,6,opt,name=updated_at,json=updatedAt,proto3" json:"updated_at,omitempty"`
	Variants     []*Variant             `protobuf:"bytes,7,rep,name=variants,proto3" json:"variants,omitempty"`
	NamespaceKey string                 `protobuf:"bytes,8,opt,name=namespace_key,json=namespaceKey,proto3" json:"namespace_key,omitempty"`
	Type         FlagType               `protobuf:"varint,9,opt,name=type,proto3,enum=flipt.FlagType" json:"type,omitempty"`
}

func (x *Flag) Reset() {
	*x = Flag{}
	if protoimpl.UnsafeEnabled {
		mi := &file_flipt_proto_msgTypes[11]
		ms := protoimpl.X.MessageStateOf(protoimpl.Pointer(x))
		ms.StoreMessageInfo(mi)
	}
}

	return protoimpl.X.MessageStringOf(x)
}

    31→func NewEvaluator(logger *zap.Logger, store Storer) *Evaluator {
    32→	return &Evaluator{
    33→		logger: logger,
    34→		store:  store,
    35→	}
    36→}

    39→	// Flag should be of variant type by default. However, for maximum backwards compatibility
    40→	// on this layer, we will check against the integer value of the flag type.
    41→	if int(flag.Type) != 0 || flag.Type != flipt.FlagType_VARIANT_FLAG_TYPE {
    42→		resp = &flipt.EvaluationResponse{}
    43→		resp.Reason = flipt.EvaluationReason_ERROR_EVALUATION_REASON
    44→		return resp, errs.ErrInvalidf("flag type %s invalid", flag.Type)
    45→	}

    60→func (s *Server) variant(ctx context.Context, flag *flipt.Flag, r *rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest) (*rpcevaluation.VariantEvaluationResponse, error) {
    61→	resp, err := s.evaluator.Evaluate(ctx, flag, r)
    62→	if err != nil {
    63→		return nil, err
    64→	}
    65→
    66→	var reason rpcevaluation.EvaluationReason
    67→
    68→	switch resp.Reason {
    69→	case flipt.EvaluationReason_MATCH_EVALUATION_REASON:
    70→		reason = rpcevaluation.EvaluationReason_MATCH_EVALUATION_REASON
    71→	case flipt.EvaluationReason_FLAG_DISABLED_EVALUATION_REASON:
    72→		reason = rpcevaluation.EvaluationReason_FLAG_DISABLED_EVALUATION_REASON
    73→	default:
    74→		reason = rpcevaluation.EvaluationReason_UNKNOWN_EVALUATION_REASON
    75→	}
    76→
    77→	ver := &rpcevaluation.VariantEvaluationResponse{
    78→		RequestId:         r.RequestId,
    79→		Match:             resp.Match,
    80→		Reason:            reason,
    81→		VariantKey:        resp.Value,
    82→		VariantAttachment: resp.Attachment,
    83→		FlagKey:           resp.FlagKey,
    84→	}
    85→
    86→	if len(resp.SegmentKeys) > 0 {
    87→		ver.SegmentKeys = resp.SegmentKeys
    88→	}
    89→
    90→	// Determine segment match type based on which rule matched
    91→	if resp.Match && len(resp.SegmentKeys) > 0 {
    92→		rules, err := s.store.GetEvaluationRules(ctx, storage.NewResource(r.NamespaceKey, r.FlagKey, storage.WithReference(r.Reference)))
    93→		if err == nil {
    94→			segmentMatchType := determineSegmentMatchType(resp.SegmentKeys, rules)
    95→			ver.SegmentMatchType = segmentMatchType
    96→		}
    97→	}
    98→
    99→	return ver, nil
   100→}

88-assistanttool_useRead
89-usertool_resultRead
   328→// determineSegmentMatchType determines whether a segment match used ALL (AND) or ANY (OR) operator
   329→// based on which rule's segments were matched.
   330→func determineSegmentMatchType(matchedSegmentKeys []string, rules []*storage.EvaluationRule) string {
   331→	if len(matchedSegmentKeys) == 0 {
   332→		return ""
   333→	}
   334→
   335→	// Create a set of matched segment keys for quick lookup
   336→	matchedSet := make(map[string]bool)
   337→	for _, key := range matchedSegmentKeys {
   338→		matchedSet[key] = true
   339→	}
   340→
   341→	// Find the rule that matches these segments
   342→	for _, rule := range rules {
   343→		ruleSegmentSet := make(map[string]bool)
   344→		for segmentKey := range rule.Segments {
   345→			ruleSegmentSet[segmentKey] = true
   346→		}
   347→
   348→		// Check if the matched segments exactly match the rule's segments
   349→		if len(ruleSegmentSet) != len(matchedSet) {
   350→			continue
   351→		}
   352→
   353→		allMatch := true
   354→		for key := range matchedSet {
   355→			if !ruleSegmentSet[key] {
   356→				allMatch = false
   357→				break
   358→			}
   359→		}
   360→
   361→		if allMatch {
   362→			// Found the matching rule, return the operator
   363→			switch rule.SegmentOperator {
   364→			case flipt.SegmentOperator_AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR:
   365→				return "ALL"
   366→			case flipt.SegmentOperator_OR_SEGMENT_OPERATOR:
   367→				return "ANY"
   368→			}
   369→			break
   370→		}
   371→	}
   372→
   373→	return ""
   374→}
   375→

Excellent! All tests pass and the code compiles successfully. Let me create a summary of the changes made:

## Summary of Changes

I've successfully implemented the `segment_match_type` field for Flipt's evaluation responses. Here's what was implemented:

### 1. **Proto Schema** (`/workspace/rpc/flipt/evaluation/evaluation.proto`)
Added `string segment_match_type = 10;` to the `VariantEvaluationResponse` message, using the next sequential tag.

### 2. **Generated Go Code** (`/workspace/rpc/flipt/evaluation/evaluation.pb.go`)
- Added `SegmentMatchType string` field to the `VariantEvaluationResponse` struct with proper protobuf tags
- Added the `GetSegmentMatchType()` getter method following the standard pattern

### 3. **Server Code** (`/workspace/internal/server/evaluation/evaluation.go`)
- Modified the `variant()` method to populate the `SegmentMatchType` field after evaluation
- Added `determineSegmentMatchType()` helper function that:
  - Finds which rule matched by comparing its segments against the returned segment keys
  - Returns `"ALL"` for AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR (all constraints matched)
  - Returns `"ANY"` for OR_SEGMENT_OPERATOR (at least one constraint matched)  
  - Returns empty string if no match found

### How It Works
1. The evaluator processes rules and matches segments using AND/OR logic
2. When a match occurs, the segment keys are returned in the evaluation response
3. The variant method calls the helper function which:
   - Builds a map of matched segment keys
   - Iterates through rules to find which one's segments match exactly
   - Returns the corresponding operator type as a string
4. This value is set on the `VariantEvaluationResponse` and returned to clients

✅ Code builds successfully

        "+",
        "+// determineSegmentMatchType determines whether a segment match used ALL (AND) or ANY (OR) operator",
        "+// based on which rule's segments were matched.",
        "+func determineSegmentMatchType(matchedSegmentKeys []string, rules []*storage.EvaluationRule) string {",
        "+  if len(matchedSegmentKeys) == 0 {",
        "+    return \"\"",
        "+  }",
        "+",
        "+  // Create a set of matched segment keys for quick lookup",
        "+  matchedSet := make(map[string]bool)",
        "+  for _, key := range matchedSegmentKeys {",
        "+    matchedSet[key] = true",
        "+  }",
        "+",
        "+  // Find the rule that matches these segments",
        "+  for _, rule := range rules {",
        "+    ruleSegmentSet := make(map[string]bool)",
        "+    for segmentKey := range rule.Segments {",
        "+      ruleSegmentSet[segmentKey] = true",
        "+    }",
        "+",
        "+    // Check if the matched segments exactly match the rule's segments",
        "+    if len(ruleSegmentSet) != len(matchedSet) {",
        "+      continue",
        "+    }",
        "+",
        "+    allMatch := true",
        "+    for key := range matchedSet {",
        "+      if !ruleSegmentSet[key] {",
        "+        allMatch = false",
        "+        break",
        "+      }",
        "+    }",
        "+",
        "+    if allMatch {",
        "+      // Found the matching rule, return the operator",
        "+      switch rule.SegmentOperator {",
        "+      case flipt.SegmentOperator_AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR:",
        "+        return \"ALL\"",
        "+      case flipt.SegmentOperator_OR_SEGMENT_OPERATOR:",
        "+        return \"ANY\"",
        "+      }",
        "+      break",
        "+    }",
        "+  }",
        "+",
        "+  return \"\"",
        "+}"

4. EDIT /workspace/internal/server/evaluation/evaluation.go
Before
func (s *Server) variant(ctx context.Context, flag *flipt.Flag, r *rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest) (*rpcevaluation.VariantEvaluationResponse, error) {
	resp, err := s.evaluator.Evaluate(ctx, flag, r)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	var reason rpcevaluation.EvaluationReason

	switch resp.Reason {
	case flipt.EvaluationReason_MATCH_EVALUATION_REASON:
		reason = rpcevaluation.EvaluationReason_MATCH_EVALUATION_REASON
	case flipt.EvaluationReason_FLAG_DISABLED_EVALUATION_REASON:
		reason = rpcevaluation.EvaluationReason_FLAG_DISABLED_EVALUATION_REASON
	default:
		reason = rpcevaluation.EvaluationReason_UNKNOWN_EVALUATION_REASON
	}

	ver := &rpcevaluation.VariantEvaluationResponse{
		RequestId:         r.RequestId,
		Match:             resp.Match,
		Reason:            reason,
		VariantKey:        resp.Value,
		VariantAttachment: resp.Attachment,
		FlagKey:           resp.FlagKey,
	}

	if len(resp.SegmentKeys) > 0 {
		ver.SegmentKeys = resp.SegmentKeys
	}

	return ver, nil
}
After
func (s *Server) variant(ctx context.Context, flag *flipt.Flag, r *rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest) (*rpcevaluation.VariantEvaluationResponse, error) {
	resp, err := s.evaluator.Evaluate(ctx, flag, r)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	var reason rpcevaluation.EvaluationReason

	switch resp.Reason {
	case flipt.EvaluationReason_MATCH_EVALUATION_REASON:
		reason = rpcevaluation.EvaluationReason_MATCH_EVALUATION_REASON
	case flipt.EvaluationReason_FLAG_DISABLED_EVALUATION_REASON:
		reason = rpcevaluation.EvaluationReason_FLAG_DISABLED_EVALUATION_REASON
	default:
		reason = rpcevaluation.EvaluationReason_UNKNOWN_EVALUATION_REASON
	}

	ver := &rpcevaluation.VariantEvaluationResponse{
		RequestId:         r.RequestId,
		Match:             resp.Match,
		Reason:            reason,
		VariantKey:        resp.Value,
		VariantAttachment: resp.Attachment,
		FlagKey:           resp.FlagKey,
	}

	if len(resp.SegmentKeys) > 0 {
		ver.SegmentKeys = resp.SegmentKeys
	}

	// Determine segment match type based on which rule matched
	if resp.Match && len(resp.SegmentKeys) > 0 {
		rules, err := s.store.GetEvaluationRules(ctx, storage.NewResource(r.NamespaceKey, r.FlagKey, storage.WithReference(r.Reference)))
		if err == nil {
			segmentMatchType := determineSegmentMatchType(resp.SegmentKeys, rules)
			ver.SegmentMatchType = segmentMatchType
		}
	}

	return ver, nil
}

// determineSegmentMatchType determines whether a segment match used ALL (AND) or ANY (OR) operator
// based on which rule's segments were matched.
func determineSegmentMatchType(matchedSegmentKeys []string, rules []*storage.EvaluationRule) string {
	if len(matchedSegmentKeys) == 0 {
		return ""
	}

	// Create a set of matched segment keys for quick lookup
	matchedSet := make(map[string]bool)
	for _, key := range matchedSegmentKeys {
		matchedSet[key] = true
	}

	// Find the rule that matches these segments
	for _, rule := range rules {
		ruleSegmentSet := make(map[string]bool)
		for segmentKey := range rule.Segments {
			ruleSegmentSet[segmentKey] = true
		}

		// Check if the matched segments exactly match the rule's segments
		if len(ruleSegmentSet) != len(matchedSet) {
			continue
		}

		allMatch := true
		for key := range matchedSet {
			if !ruleSegmentSet[key] {
				allMatch = false
				break
			}
		}

		if allMatch {
			// Found the matching rule, return the operator
			switch rule.SegmentOperator {
			case flipt.SegmentOperator_AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR:
				return "ALL"
			case flipt.SegmentOperator_OR_SEGMENT_OPERATOR:
				return "ANY"
			}
			break
		}
	}

	return ""
}

// determineSegmentMatchType determines whether a segment match used ALL (AND) or ANY (OR) operator
// based on which rule's segments were matched.
func determineSegmentMatchType(matchedSegmentKeys []string, rules []*storage.EvaluationRule) string {
	if len(matchedSegmentKeys) == 0 {
		return ""
	}

	// Create a set of matched segment keys for quick lookup
	matchedSet := make(map[string]bool)
	for _, key := range matchedSegmentKeys {
		matchedSet[key] = true
	}

	// Find the rule that matches these segments
	for _, rule := range rules {
		ruleSegmentSet := make(map[string]bool)
		for segmentKey := range rule.Segments {
			ruleSegmentSet[segmentKey] = true
		}

		// Check if the matched segments exactly match the rule's segments
		if len(ruleSegmentSet) != len(matchedSet) {
			continue
		}

		allMatch := true
		for key := range matchedSet {
			if !ruleSegmentSet[key] {
				allMatch = false
				break
			}
		}

		if allMatch {
			// Found the matching rule, return the operator
			switch rule.SegmentOperator {
			case flipt.SegmentOperator_AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR:
				return "ALL"
			case flipt.SegmentOperator_OR_SEGMENT_OPERATOR:
				return "ANY"
			}
			break
		}
	}

	return ""
}
